Conclusion of the Fourth Plenary Session 21

Yu Youren Reads the Declaration

Chiang Kai-shek Delivers the Closing Address

(Nanjing) The Fourth Plenary Session was held on the morning of the 23rd. First, an expanded memorial week was held, with the participation of central and national government staff, presided over by Cai Yuanpei. After the ceremony, Dai Chuanxian reported. After a ten-minute break, the closing ceremony was held, presided over by Enkebatu. The order was as follows: (1) All stand at attention; (2) Play music; (3) Sing the party song; (4) Bow three times to the portrait of the Premier; (5) The chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will; (6) Silent tribute for three minutes; (7) Read the General Assembly Declaration (read by Yu Youren); (8) Chiang Kai-shek delivers the closing speech, and then shouts: 1. All party comrades unite; 2. All the people of the country unite to build; 3. Down with Japanese imperialism; 4. Long live the Chinese Nationalist Party; 5. Long live the Republic of China; 6. Three cheers for the Three Principles of the People. Then play music, take pictures, and end the meeting. (Special dispatch from the 23rd)

(Nanjing) Chiang Kai-shek delivered a closing speech at the closing ceremony of the Fourth Plenary Session this morning. The original text is as follows:

Chairman, fellow comrades, today the Fourth National Congress is adjourned. The Presidium asked me to deliver the closing speech. As we close this meeting, we recall the Premier's speech at the closing of the First National Congress. The Premier said, "The struggle of party members is the same as the struggle of the army..." You have held a ten-day meeting here, and decided on many proposals. After the adjournment, you must bring them back to your local areas, distribute them to the comrades in your locality, and go to fight separately. Therefore, this conference is like a military conference, which has set various battle plans and handed them over to the generals to bring back for implementation. Simply put, our party members are like soldiers, and should act in unison and fight separately according to the battle plan set by the general headquarters. Today, we restate this precise lesson of the Premier as our closing speech. This time, when the country is plagued by internal and external troubles, especially when the spirit of the party is scattered and separated and people's hearts are shaken, the comrades of our Fourth National Congress, no matter how bizarre the rumors were before the meeting, and how complex the tricks of slander and alienation were, we adhered to a sincere love for the party and the country, established our confidence, and jointly completed the mission of the Fourth National Congress. I dare to say that this spirit of loving the party, loving the country, being loyal, and not being confused deserves to be a true believer of the Premier and can be worthy of the country and the people. We can hold this meeting and realize the unity of the party in the midst of disintegration, regardless of everything. This spirit is greater than anything else. Now we have closed the meeting. As for how to strive for the party and the country, our plans and policies have been determined. According to the Premier's words, if the party is compared to the army, the National Congress is the general headquarters, that is, the commander-in-chief of the whole country. Since we have the great responsibility of saving the party and saving the country, our National Congress must swear to fight to the death for the general public and the party. Now the closing words are no different from a mobilization speech. In this environment of internal and external troubles, our congress is like Zhuge Liang when he presented the "Chushi Biao" (Memorial on Dispatching the Army). The Premier said that in the past, in the imperial era, there was only one emperor. Now that the Republic of China has been established, sovereignty rests with the people. Therefore, today's 400 million compatriots are all emperors. Our Chinese Nationalist Party must take responsibility for these 400 million emperors to save the country and save the masters. Zhuge Liang's "Chushi Biao" is full of loyalty and grief. Now we are in Zhuge Liang's position. We must take responsibility for the 400 million masters to save the country. Everyone is clear about the environment in which our country and our party are now. At this time of severe natural disasters and people's livelihood is meager, Japanese imperialists are invading our territory and trampling on our country with powerful military force. This is truly a great disaster for our country and the greatest shame for our people. If we ourselves cannot unite and work together to fight against foreign enemies, the demise of the party and the country is imminent. I often say that our greatest disaster is not in foreign enemies. If we Chinese, especially Chinese party members, can be self-reliant, self-strengthening, and spiritually united, even if there are ten Japans, they cannot shake our country. Now we want to ask, is this foreign trouble because we are self-reliant and self-strengthening and are being invaded? This answer does not need me to elaborate. In short, our National Congress this time has absolutely no phenomenon of power struggle. We are doing our best to seek unity within the party and to defend against foreign aggression and save our country. We are not afraid of any powerful enemy, but only ask how we are and how the party's strength and spirit are. We must carefully examine ourselves and work together in politics and military affairs to seek long-term progress. The ancients said, "People must insult themselves before others insult them, and people must attack themselves before others attack them." This sentence can be our teaching. Yue Fei of the Song Dynasty was trapped by the Jin people, not because Yue Fei's combat ability was weak, but because he was jealous of the traitor Qin Hui in the rear, which led to the failure of his achievements. When Yue Fei was fighting hard and winning on the front line, the rear suddenly issued twelve gold medals ordering him to withdraw his troops. When we think of this, we feel that if the Chinese Nationalist Party wants to be determined to save the country, it is necessary to unify the country and concentrate its forces, especially to ensure that there are no traitors like Qin Hui in the rear to hinder or slander us, so as to achieve the goal of resisting foreign aggression. If we want to be responsible for saving the country, and some people not only do not want us to save the country, but also want to slander and frame us in various ways, then in addition to all the worries, there will be a serious difficulty. Our situation is now unfortunately showing this phenomenon. We must break through difficulties from countless restraints and slanderous layers to shoulder the responsibility of resisting foreign aggression. This requires the earnest attention of all representatives. The Premier once said that the United States has only one Washington, but this one Washington must be created by countless anonymous Washingtons. Now that we are in this situation of internal and external attacks and heavy difficulties, we can only sacrifice regardless of success or failure, with our sincerity, to save the country and resist foreign aggression. We want to use countless unnamed Yue Wumus to create a Yue Wumu of the Republic of China. We have nothing else to rely on today for the party and the country. We can only take a sincere heart like Zhuge Wuhou's determination to devote ourselves to the task until our death to repay the Premier and the people of the whole country. Because of the many problems in the country, everyone is very busy at this National Congress. Perhaps some of you comrades feel that there are some shortcomings in the spirit and discipline of the party. There may even be sadness, sighing, and unspeakable pain in the venue. This is not only the case for you, but also for me personally. But we must know that the spirit of loyalty and sincerity of this National Congress is more important than any other. From the 13th year of the Republic of China to today, the degree of danger of the country has never been like today. We gathered together in this unprecedented difficult situation to hold this meeting, so that our party can unite, so that the people know that we only care about the country's difficulties and not our selfishness, especially in this time of crisis, showing that we can express absolute magnanimity and painstaking efforts to seek the unity of the party to resist foreign aggression. We can express this spirit. In this point, it is the greatest success of the congress. In the past, after each national congress, I always felt a little uneasy. But when we close the meeting today, we can say that we are worthy of the Premier and the people. We really feel at ease and have no regrets. We are now working hard to move forward according to the resolutions of the congress. This time, we unanimously sacrificed everything and sought perfection in everything. In the very difficult situation of the party and the country, we completed our responsibilities and were able to take the Premier's heart as our heart and the Premier's will as our will. This is a matter worthy of special mention in the revolutionary history of the party. Therefore, we should not be discouraged. We have done our best to be loyal to the party and to the country. We can then take on the great task of saving the country without hesitation. Zhuge Liang used "devote oneself to the task until death" as his oath, and Yue Wumu used "loyalty to the country" as his oath. These are the common maxims of our party members and also the two firm oaths we tell the people of the whole country. Fellow representatives, we must all know that to this day, we can only carry forward our revolutionary morality and revolutionary spirit. The party members of the Chinese Nationalist Party want to save the country and save the masters. Not only do they want to be Zhuge Liang, but they also want to prepare to be Yue Wumu. Only in this way can they be worthy of the Premier's believers and live up to the mission of the Fourth National Congress. (Special dispatch from the 23rd)

Everyone was able to be faithful, loyal, diligent, and cautious in deciding the national policy of resisting foreign aggression and internal unity. This is a fortunate thing for the future of the country and the nation. Buy knowledge and ability to dedicate to duties and careers, and establish a solid foundation. Under the guidance of the two principles of restoring inherent morality and intelligence and catching up with world culture, seek improvement and progress. If we waste one minute of our time and energy on our own enjoyment, the duties and occupations will suffer a minute of loss. If we waste knowledge and ability for our own sake, our doctrine and policy will lose one minute of strength. Therefore, being loyal to our duties is the real way to save the country. Day by day, the causes of danger became deeper and deeper, until we encountered this national crisis of internal and external troubles, natural disasters, and man-made disasters at the same time. At this time, we must revitalize our spirit and strive forward, and at the same time, we must earnestly reflect. Now the task has been completed. The future Fifth National Congress will definitely be able to show the good results created by the united unity of all party comrades and compatriots. (Special dispatch from the 23rd)

Declaration of the Fourth Plenary Session 22

(Nanjing) The full text of the Declaration of the Fourth Plenary Session is as follows: Since the Third National Congress of the Party, two years and eight months have passed. During this period, what the Party and the people of the whole country have worked together to achieve is the construction of the tutelage period and the consolidation of the foundation of peaceful unification. However, obstacles have multiplied, and the Party and the country have suffered many misfortunes, causing immeasurable sacrifices to the people's livelihood and national strength. The work of tutelage has not been realized as expected. Until May of this year, the National Conference was convened to formulate the Provisional Constitution for the Period of Political Tutelage, which means that from now on, all citizens of the country and the Party shall be able to work together in accordance with the publicly established norms. When the national army was engaged in the suppression of the Red Bandits in Gan and E, the country encountered an unprecedented flood, with displacement and death all over the field, and the whole country cried out and devoted all its efforts to relief work. At this time, the tyrannical Japan took advantage of our crisis and carried out its invasion, forcibly occupied our land, massacred our people, bombed our cities, and colluded with traitors and bandits to destroy the integrity of our country with continuous acts of violence. The depth of the national crisis is extremely serious. The Congress was held during this period of serious national crisis, and it is believed that if our Chinese nation does not seek a way to survive with the determination to die, the nation will be plunged into eternal demise. If the comrades of the Party cannot unite and fully shoulder the heavy responsibility of saving the country and swear to lead the way, the revolutionary cause will be cut off from now on. In this autumn of crisis, we express our utmost sincerity in the basic essentials to our comrades and compatriots throughout the country.

The Premier said, "We must unite 400 million people into a large nation and build a strong and substantial country based on the Three Principles of the People in order to survive in today's world." The truth of saving the country lies only in this. Therefore, if we want to seek the unity of the whole country, we must first start with the real unity of the Party. Any country,

Page 8

When the country is reviving and building, all the people's minds and the revolutionary central forces are firmly united, and there is no failure. On the contrary, there is no failure. Today, we will try to conduct a frank inspection. We dare to say that the people of the whole country's belief in the Three Principles of the People has not changed for a long time, but their expectations for the Party have gradually faded. This undeniable phenomenon is due to the scattered and separated signs within the Party, which are painful to the people, and also due to the failure of the comrades of the Party to win the love and respect of the people through arduous practical work. Now, when the national crisis is serious, it is an opportunity for self-reflection and self-redemption. The Congress takes the Premier's heart as its heart and the Premier's will as its will, eliminates all past alienation, and strives for the sincere unity of the Party. All our comrades should be of one mind and one heart, restore mutual trust, forgive each other for their faults, encourage each other for their hard work, follow the Premier's instructions to sacrifice freedom and contribute their abilities, create an unshakable spiritual unity, let our hair down and wear our crowns, and resist foreign aggression together. Then we can thank the people and relieve the national crisis. At the same time, we must also thoroughly examine the mistakes of past work, prevent the shortcomings of being scattered and following the old ways, attaching importance to form and neglecting practice, and take sacrifice as an advocate for the whole country at any time and place, take action as the first in the world, take loyalty to our duties as the only responsibility to implement the doctrine and achieve the purpose of saving the country and saving the people, establish the determination to give our lives in times of danger, and express the basic morality of revolutionaries. Then the people's respect for the Party will definitely become more and more intense, reversing the national destiny in times of danger, and expecting the realization of the doctrine. It is not the responsibility of others to turn misfortune into blessing. This is what the Congress is willing to tell our comrades in the Party. In modern times, the foundation of a country lies in the consolidation of unity and the enrichment of national strength. It also depends on the people's determination to be brave and enterprising, to establish a common belief and to work together to achieve it. The Premier's Great Program of National Construction and the Strategy of National Construction, which he left to us, are the highest principles for maintaining national survival. With painstaking efforts, we hope that our successors will succeed. However, for several years, the actual effectiveness of construction has not been obvious, and the increase in national strength is still rare. Recently, there has been an unprecedented foreign invasion. The Party is sincerely responsible for the failures of our compatriots to the Party. And what we will thank our country for in the future is only to do our best to sacrifice together with our compatriots to save the country and resist foreign aggression. We firmly believe that with the concerted efforts of our country, we will be able to overcome any difficulties and maintain the security of the country. Only our compatriots, who have shared the dangers of the country, will certainly be able to examine the great responsibility, respond to changes and resist foreign aggression. We must have the spirit of sacrificing individuals to preserve the whole group, and fundamentally, we must take action to create real strength. Looking at the history of various countries in the world, the traces of rising and revitalizing the old do not take extreme hardship, take double labor, and donate individual freedom and rights to contribute to the country's proposals. These arduous and arduous efforts to catch up are the spirit that our country must learn from. The Congress believes that the construction of the country in the future must start from the three aspects of military affairs, education, and economy, and make a thorough and vigorous transformation of both material and spiritual aspects, sweeping away the mentality of luck, creating a solid national defense, and ensuring the permanent survival of the nation. We earnestly hope that all our comrades in the Party will abide by the resolutions, work hard, unite our compatriots across the country, implement national mobilization, and complete the great task of our national construction with a consistent step and the greatest determination. The Congress firmly believes that the revitalization of the national spirit will be the most difficult time for the country. Only when the country is in the most difficult time can it fully express and test the national self-confidence. May all our compatriots and comrades throughout the country dedicate their loyalty and courage, concentrate under the Three Principles of the People, and make active preparations to save the country. Externally, we must defend against aggression, defend national rights, and strive for international justice and peace, and strive for the right to national survival and self-defense. The temporary gains and losses are not to be counted, and all sacrifices are not to be cherished. Humanity will not be destroyed, civilization will not be destroyed, and the final victory will belong to us. Internally, we must revitalize politics, strive for construction, move forward at the same time, and have no regrets, in order to establish the foundation for the permanent independence and self-reliance of the Chinese nation, which is also to maintain the permanent survival and prosperity of the Chinese nation. All our comrades should know that saving the country is to save the Party. All our compatriots throughout the country should be able to share the contribution of all our spiritual and material strength to obey the command of the central government, and there is no way to reverse the national crisis and fulfill the responsibility of saving the country. This is what we say. (Special dispatch from the 23rd)

Gu Weijun Acts as Minister of Foreign Affairs 24

Government Order Issued, Assumes Office Today

(Nanjing) The National Government ordered on the 23rd that Gu Weijun be appointed as Acting Minister of Foreign Affairs. This order, (Special dispatch from the 23rd)

(Nanjing) After the order for Gu Weijun to act as Minister of Foreign Affairs was issued, Li Gu planned to go to the ministry to assume office on the 24th. (Special dispatch from the 23rd)

(Nanjing) Minister of Foreign Affairs Shi Zhaoji is currently attending the League of Nations and is temporarily unable to return to China. Changchuan is stationed in the ministry. The government specially appointed Gu Weijun as Acting Minister of Foreign Affairs on the 23rd. The appointment was sent from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to the Huilong Hotel for Gu to accept. Gu has recently been personally involved in diplomatic documents and has been the de facto Minister of Foreign Affairs. The government has given him an appointment to show respect for the foreign affairs relationship. Gu told the interviewer that the League of Nations is looking for an appropriate solution to the Sino-Japanese incident. Our side firmly requests the use of Articles 15 and 16 of the Covenant of the League of Nations. It is expected that the League of Nations will not ignore our country's legitimate demands. He also said that the general public believes that if the League of Nations does not have a satisfactory solution, our country can withdraw from the League of Nations. In fact, according to the Charter of the League of Nations, any participating country that wishes to withdraw must notify two years in advance. It is not possible to withdraw immediately upon notification. As for another method, according to the Washington Nine-Power Treaty, you can request that the documents of the dispute between the two countries be publicly announced and an international conference be convened to find a solution based on the Nine-Power Treaty. Gu will be able to go to the ministry to take up his new position within days. (Special dispatch from the 23rd)

(Nanjing) Gu Weijun is scheduled to go to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 24th to take up his post first. (Special dispatch from the 23rd)

(Paris) Gu Weijun's appointment as Acting Minister of Foreign Affairs has had a very good impression in the League of Nations and diplomatic circles. Gu has a prominent reputation in the League of Nations, and diplomatic circles feel that Gu can use his gentle forces to promote good relations between China and Japan. (Reuters dispatch from the 23rd)

贛榆股匪肆擾 29

Bandits Run Rampant in Ganyu:

係受日浪人鼓煽

Instigated by Japanese Ronin

匪中高揭旭日旗

Bandits Raise the Rising Sun Flag

(Xuzhou) Maritime News: A large group of maritime bandits, instigated by Japanese ronin, captured Linmatuan and Huangniyai in Ganyu County on the 17th. The bandits raised the Rising Sun Flag. It is reported that they were bought by the Japanese to disrupt our coastal defenses. These bandits previously attacked Liujiashagou, causing severe arson and looting. The troops stationed in Qingkou by Liu Guoming, the 95th Brigade Commander, rushed to repel them. They are now being incited to cause further disturbances. Government troops and police units have gone to encircle and suppress them, and the bandits are fleeing towards the coast. (23rd Dispatch)

(Xuzhou) Maritime News: The bandits Liu Dashui, Wei Lianmiao, and others who had entrenched themselves in Longjuzhen have been suppressed and defeated by the troops of the 95th Brigade under Liu Guoming stationed in Hai. Over 50 bandits were killed, and over 20 were captured alive and executed on the spot. More than 10 hostages were rescued. The remaining bandits fled towards Bowangzhen. Longju has been cleared. (23rd Dispatch)

The final League of Nations sanction against Japan is economic blockade, which is theoretically certain. However: 1. Due to the poor economic conditions of European countries after the war, they are expanding trade to try to recover, and they may not be able to afford to suffer considerable losses from an economic blockade against Japan for the sake of China. 2. The League of Nations itself has only been established for a few years, and its foundation is not solid. It can only issue fair theories on international affairs. Because of its insufficient strength, it cannot in fact blockade Japan. 3. International disputes between the strong and the weak are easier to resolve. However, when one is strong and one is weak, the League of Nations finds it quite difficult. If it cannot stop Japan this time, it will lose credibility, and the League of Nations may fundamentally shake because no one supports it. As for Japan's occupation of the Northeast, although it is complacent, it has suffered a great moral loss. Moreover, the troops it sent to the Northeast, it declares were only over 10,000, but it certainly did not send troops from within the country, only from Korea. Its actual strength is also limited and it seems it cannot have ambitions elsewhere. The United States signed the Nine-Power Treaty and is trying its best to help China, but as it is not a member of the League of Nations, it has difficulty speaking out. (23rd Dispatch)

No Possibility of a Coalition Cabinet

Japan Associated Press, Tokyo, 23rd: Home Minister Adachi's statement is like throwing a stone into the calm political sea, suddenly causing a great shock. Many in Japanese political circles are viewing the current cabinet as brewing a major crisis and are worried about its fate. Former Finance Minister Inukai, who had been touring Kyushu's hot springs for recuperation since mid-month, also arrived in Tokyo on the evening of the 21st. Amidst this political upheaval, Inukai's actions are attracting much attention.

Another Telegram: Home Minister Adachi conferred with party executives at his private residence today regarding a coalition cabinet, telling those around him that the only way to resolve the current difficult situation is to organize a coalition cabinet. My belief has not changed at all. Those who oppose the coalition cabinet must not be nationals. There are no prejudices between the Prime Minister and me. As for how to realize my ideals, we still need to calmly observe the development of the situation.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 23rd: Since Home Minister Adachi issued his statement, the government and the party have been greatly shaken. Seiyukai Secretary-General Kuhara visited Saionji in Okitsu yesterday to inform him that Adachi's proposal to organize a coalition cabinet was to solve the current difficulties, and explained the Seiyukai's attitude, seeking Saionji's understanding. All cabinet members felt that it seems impossible to organize a coalition cabinet at the present time.

法政治家洛歇逝世 58

French Politician Loucheur Passes Away

Havas News Agency, Paris, 22nd: Former French Minister of State Loucheur passed away at 2:30 p.m. today at the age of 59. In recent years, Loucheur has made considerable contributions to negotiations with Germany and legislation on social issues. Upon hearing the news, the French President immediately sent condolences to his family. Loucheur was a technician who had always been involved in industry. During the European War, he joined the cabinet, serving successively in the departments of military equipment and industrial recovery. In 1921, Loucheur and German Reconstruction Minister Rathenau signed the so-called Wiesbaden Agreement. In 1925, he participated in the negotiation of the Locarno Treaties. He made considerable efforts during parliamentary discussions on social insurance law.

Japanese Military Propaganda to Occupy Harbin

Damei Evening News, Harbin, 21st: Based on recent conversations between Japanese military officers, it seems that the Japanese army is not satisfied with occupying Qiqihar and is about to occupy Harbin. A certain newspaper here published a statement by Japanese Kwantung Army Commander Honjō, who reportedly said, "I am very troubled by the situation in Harbin. Therefore, there may be a need to dispatch troops to occupy it. I am closely observing Harbin. If there are disturbances that endanger the lives and property of Japanese residents, then I am prepared to send troops there." Since occupying Qiqihar and Changchun, the Japanese military's position allows it to quickly dispatch troops to Harbin when necessary. Furthermore, Japanese General Doihara also told this newspaper's (Damei Evening News) reporter last night that whether or not to send Japanese troops to Harbin is still uncertain, but that they will dispatch troops if necessary. Today, Japanese Consul General Ohashi protested to the local authorities about two matters: one was the boycott of Japanese goods, and the other was that Ding Chao, the Commander of the China Eastern Railway Protection Army, allowed scattered soldiers from Qiqihar to enter Harbin. However, Ohashi said that the situation in Harbin has improved somewhat on the whole since the Japanese military occupied Qiqihar. He hopes that it will not be necessary to send Japanese troops here. (Note: Harbin is the hub of the China Eastern Railway and has the power to control the northern part of the three northeastern provinces. If the Japanese military occupies it, then its infringement on Russian interests will become even more obvious. Therefore, this move is highly noteworthy in future Japanese-Russian relations.) According to the reporter's observation, the situation in Harbin is mostly in the hands of Zhang Jinghui. Zhang has always been known for being pro-Japanese. Since the Mukden Incident, Zhang has obtained a large number of guns and ammunition, reportedly all seized by the Japanese military from the Shenyang Arsenal. He is currently using these to train security forces, who are drilling diligently every day. If Zhang can use these security forces to control everything and indirectly serve the Japanese, then Japanese troops may not need to come. However, the local people, the Kuomintang, and other factions are opposing Zhang and unwilling to surrender. Therefore, the future of Harbin is still uncertain.

Tianjin Rioters Disturb Again 60

Tianjin Correspondence: Besides the Japanese Concession, Tianjin has been quite calm in recent days. All shops have reopened, and traffic has resumed. It is hoped that the city will return to its former state soon. However, yesterday around noon, a dozen or so thugs in the Xiguangkai and Caochang'an areas attempted to cause trouble. The authorities discovered this and sent security teams. The thugs fled at the sight of the teams. A temporary curfew was imposed yesterday afternoon, and the situation returned to normal after an hour. However, the Japanese have not slightly withdrawn their vigilance, and they have not returned the two districts and six police stations that they forcibly occupied. It is also reported that the Japanese warship "Kari" carrying more than 2,000 marines arrived at Tanggu, but could not sail to Tianjin due to shallow water. The marines, due to strict surveillance by various countries, could not disembark at Tanggu. They have now changed into civilian clothes, formed groups of three to five, and secretly arrived in Tianjin by car. They are expected to arrive in full force within the next few days. The latest situation is recorded as follows:

Thugs Caused Disturbance for Half an Hour After the Chinese area of ​​the city implemented the withdrawal of defenses on the 18th at the request of the Japanese side, the serious atmosphere of war preparations in the Japanese Concession has never diminished. Late the day before, Japanese troops stationed at Haiguang Temple, Nan Shi Pai Lou and other places frequently fired live ammunition at the Chinese area to provoke incidents. At 12:10 noon yesterday (20th),

The Japanese side again incited more than 60 plainclothes thugs, divided into left and right routes, to go to the Xiguangkai Yan Hai Hui area to fire guns and cause disturbances. The 16th and 19th Squadrons of our security forces, upon hearing the news, went together to round them up. For a time, gunfire erupted, sounding like a string of pearls. The shopkeepers panicked and closed their doors one after another. After about twenty minutes, the thugs lost contact and scattered like birds and beasts. A pedestrian, about thirty years old, was shot and killed by a stray bullet near a certain lumberyard. Zhang Wenzong, a rickshaw puller, was also shot in the left leg by a plainclothes team, bleeding profusely. He was taken to the Municipal Hospital for treatment that day. The local authorities, in order to prevent them from taking advantage of the situation again, have increased police forces in the area to eliminate them. At the same time, the glass doors and windows of the police station in Caochang'an, Nanmalu, were also destroyed by thugs.

Temporary Curfew in the Chinese Area When the gunfire first broke out, it was at the time when the curfew was being lifted, and the pedestrians were like weaving. Upon hearing the alarm, there was great chaos. Hebei and various special districts then announced a temporary curfew to maintain order. The Jingang and Jintang Bridges were also temporarily raised. White and red牌 trams on all routes were therefore suspended. The Italian Concession authorities redeployed defensive works at all intersections and inspected pedestrians with extreme strictness. It was not until 3:00 p.m. that it was relatively safe, and traffic also resumed. However, in the Haiguang Temple area, gunfire could still be heard from time to time at 6:00 p.m.

Two Districts and Six Stations Not Returned The two districts and six police stations outside the Nanyingmen in our city have been forcibly occupied by Japanese military police since the night of the 8th, and two weeks have passed in an instant. Our authorities have repeatedly questioned the Japanese consul, but he has never responded. The authorities, concerned about sovereignty, specially sent Shen Dijia, the chief of the diplomatic section, to visit the Japanese consul, Kuwajima, the day before yesterday to ask when they would be returned. At that time, the Japanese consul could not answer and promised to consult with the commander of the garrison, Kashii, and then reply. Yesterday, Shen met with the Japanese consul again. According to his verbal reply, the two districts and six stations would be returned immediately, but he did not mention when or what time, apparently still using cunning tricks to perfunctorily deal with the matter.

Traffic in the Japanese Concession Still Cut Off The residents of the Japanese Concession, seeing that traffic in the Chinese area has fully recovered, held a meeting of the residents' group the day before yesterday to request the resumption of traffic on Asahi Street to maintain commerce. The Japanese consul agreed and drafted an announcement to resume traffic immediately. However, due to the opposition of the commander of the garrison, it was not implemented. It is reported that the Japanese consul consulted with the commander of the garrison, Kashii, yesterday about resuming traffic on Asahi Street and allowing trams to pass. Kashii has agreed, but trams are only allowed to run from the southeast corner to the Zhongyuan Company. South of the Zhongyuan Company, traffic is still not allowed, and tram passengers must be checked by the Japanese army before they can enter the concession. Therefore, there was still no result. Therefore, the earthworks and power grids in various parts of the Japanese Concession are still set up, and Japanese troops are still patrolling at the intersection of the Chinese and Japanese boundaries. Only the French-Japanese intersection at Lichiang can be passed at will from 12:00 noon to 4:00 p.m., but it must be inspected. After 4:00 p.m., the Japanese army will again take up positions. Every night, Japanese armored vehicles patrol the intersections, showing no sign of withdrawing their defenses.

Release Time Will Be Extended Since the plainclothes team was suppressed, our authorities, in order to facilitate merchants and people, have specially stipulated the release time to allow citizens to purchase daily necessities. It was originally scheduled from 10:00 a.m. to 1:00 p.m., and then extended from 8:00 a.m. to 4:00 p.m. The market has been calm in recent days. Although there are a few scattered thugs still hiding in remote areas, the authorities have taken strict precautions and have been arrested one after another. Therefore, the public security in the city can be guaranteed to be safe. The British Secret Proposal Reported by the Japanese Newspaper 62

The Japanese Army Opposes This Case

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Denies This Matter

15th Japan: The Osaka Mainichi Shimbun disclosed a message saying that the United Kingdom has a secret proposal, which is agreed by the United Kingdom and the United States. After this news was published, many parties in Japan considered it a fact, but Shidehara resolutely denied it. Now the Paris Conference has become the focus of worldwide attention. In this tense atmosphere, the 16th when the League of Nations Council will be reopened is approaching. According to US Secretary of State Stimson, Japan's reply to the US is an extremely satisfactory and harmonious one. British opinion has recently seemed to be slightly better for Japan. So what is Japan's so-called harmonious attitude, and how is this situation caused? These two things are considered incredible by the world. The conspiracy and secret strategy of the United Kingdom have been very obvious. On the one hand, the United Kingdom supports the League of Nations, and on the other hand, it has the ambition to establish commercial rights in China. It wants to use the power of the League of Nations to oppress Japan by taking the Manchurian Incident as an opportunity. However, Japan did not yield, but instead showed a form of excitement. Therefore, the United Kingdom secretly proposed a proposal to Japan a few days ago, the terms of which are as follows: (1) The United Kingdom will hold the League of Nations Council on the 16th, with the main focus on maintaining the face of the League of Nations and Japan, and strive to solve the problem. (2) The United Kingdom will have the leader of the League of Nations speak and announce the claims made by the Japanese government on the 26th, that is, the articles centered on respecting treaties and protecting overseas Chinese, on the one hand, ask China to express its approval, and ask Japan to express its satisfaction with this approach, and immediately declare the withdrawal of troops within the Manchurian Railway. (3) Please Japan to suspend military operations in northern Manchuria, and also be careful in North China, and do not expand the dispute. (4) In order for the League of Nations Council to proceed smoothly, please Japan send Ambassador Matsudaira to Paris to contact the United Kingdom. The above proposal was not forwarded by the diplomatic organs of the United Kingdom, but was sent to the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs by special means, and an understanding seems to have been established between the United Kingdom and the United States. Ambassadors Matsudaira and Yoshida then decided to go to Paris, revealing Stimson's so-called Japan's harmonious attitude. The British Foreign Secretary once declared in Parliament [seeking US assistance], and there was a Dawes-Matsudaira-Simon three-person London meeting. The secret documents exchanged by the three countries are the above four settlement proposals. The newspaper reported that the Japanese army opposed this case, while Shidehara denied it. Shidehara's speech said that the saying that a secret agreement was established between the United Kingdom, Japan and the United States before the League of Nations Council meeting was completely untrue. The Japanese government decided to follow the previously announced policy and attend the council meeting held in Paris on the 16th, that is, (1) direct negotiations between China and Japan, China recognizes the basic outline, and after the emotional Deputy and China and Japan, then conduct troop withdrawal negotiations, (2) wait until the Manchurian local government is established and public security can be ensured, then begin troop withdrawal, therefore the Japanese government does not need to reach an understanding with any country before the meeting. The British proposal, which was sent to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs by special means without going through diplomatic organs, is also impossible. According to reports, the so-called British secret case is mostly unreliable, and judging from Shidehara's words, even if China recognizes its requirements, there is no talk of troop withdrawal, let alone implementing troop withdrawal. It can be seen that Japan's true intention is to occupy it factually and for a long time. Everything else is just embellishment.

Internal Story of the Japanese Cabinet Shaking 63

Touting a National Unity Cabinet

Tokyo Correspondence: Time flies. A year has passed since Reijiro Wakatsuki was ordered to form a cabinet. The fate of the Wakatsuki cabinet during this year has been swaying in the harsh winds and bitter rains. The world's recession is getting deeper and deeper, Japan's domestic industries are gradually declining, and fiscal revenue has been greatly reduced. Recently, the sudden rise of the UK's turmoil has further triggered the uneasiness of the Japanese financial community. The gold standard is already in motion. The outbreak of the Shenyang Incident this time caused a direct conflict between the government and the military, and international public opinion is extremely difficult to grasp, so diplomacy has fallen into an abnormal state. Under this heavy pressure, a great crisis is inevitably lurking in the future of the Wakatsuki cabinet. In such a situation of diplomatic difficulty and financial difficulty, Genji Matsuda and other first-class figures in the political world, as well as those inside and outside the government and the party, have fully exposed their determination to [disbelieve] the current cabinet, and at the same time, they are eager to have a [national unity cabinet] appear in the near future to cope with the current difficulties.

Although there is no specific expression of the movement for this national unity cabinet, the recent busy visits of Mr. Matsuda and others to Wakatsuki and Prince Saionji imply a kind of active meaning. In addition, Mr. Matsuda and others' secret efforts to win over powerful people from the Minseito and Seiyukai seem to be a very obvious symbol.

Rumors are rife. Prime Minister Wakatsuki expressed some opinions at the beginning of the meeting with cabinet ministers and party members the day before yesterday (14th), intending to sweep away the rumors and rumors from the past. [The recent situation is indeed a difficult and eventful autumn, but to solve this difficult problem, it is really indispensable for the current cabinet. The [national unity cabinet] said recently chanted inside and outside the party, in addition to hindering the international credibility of the government, it is of no benefit to the country. We should strictly prohibit this kind of rash action, and at the same time, we must work hard to move forward and deal with the current major situation well, so that we can live up to the trust of the Emperor and comfort the expectations of the people].

At that time, the government and some of the parties were very confident that this speech would be effective, and could be used to dispel some of the unease in the current situation, but in fact, there seemed to be some room for doubt. (1) The elder statesmen have recently expressed extreme disappointment with Prime Minister Wakatsuki's attitude, and at the same time, in order to open up the current situation of turmoil, they intend to make the current cabinet step down. (2) Prime Minister Wakatsuki himself seems to have a sense of [running out of steam] for the current difficulties, and at the same time, he expects that he will not be able to pass the difficult hurdle when attending the recent parliament, so he has a considerable understanding of the organization of a coalition cabinet or a cooperative cabinet. (3) There are still some major unresolved conditions regarding the relationship with the military. (4) Matsuda and others, the central figures in the slight movement of the political situation, did not attend the懇談meeting on the 14th. From these relationships, Prime Minister Wakatsuki's speech may not have any effective effect in reality, and the fate of the Wakatsuki cabinet seems to be [the end of its rope].

In short, the movement for a national unity cabinet has already taken shape. After Interior Minister Adachi returns to Beijing on the 21st, it will definitely be more superficial. However, whether the life of the Wakatsuki cabinet will eventually be, and whether the coalition cabinet will die due to difficult childbirth, depends entirely on the changes in the international situation in the future, and the safety of the future situation in the Far East is entirely linked to the ebb and flow of this Japanese coup. (Shoufa, November 16)

Opening of the Fourth National Congress of the Guangdong Province 64

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Fourth National Congress of the Kuomintang convened in Guangzhou held its opening ceremony at 9:00 a.m. on the 18th at the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall on Dexuan Road. More than a thousand people from various military, political, party, and group representatives participated in the ceremony. Members of the Extraordinary Conference, such as Sun Ke, Xiao Focheng, Deng Zhiru, Chen Jitang, Li Zongren, Jing Hengyi, Deng Qingyang, Shi Qingyang, Li Wenfan, Chen Youren, Chen Ce, Liu Jiwen, Lin Yungai, Chen Shuren, Jiao Yitang, Zhang Zhiben, Fu Rulin, Bai Yunti, etc., and members of the Guangdong Provincial Government, Tang Shaoyi, and members of the Provincial and Municipal Governments, and members of the Provincial and Municipal Party Departments all participated. More than 700 representatives attended the Fourth National Congress. At 9:20, the opening ceremony was held, presided over by Sun Ke. After the ceremony, Sun delivered an opening speech, which mainly stated the reasons and tasks for the establishment of the Extraordinary Conference, and then stated that in order to solve the current crisis of the party and the country, the Extraordinary Conference specially hurried to convene the Fourth National Congress to make the central leading organs from temporary to official, and entrust the responsibility borne by a small number of people to the organs entrusted by the whole party. Originally, the mission of the Extraordinary Conference was to eliminate the communist disaster and overthrow the dictatorship. Unfortunately, neither of these two things was achieved. Suddenly, a strong neighbor came to oppress, and the national life was in danger. In order to accept the national people's request for unity, the Extraordinary Conference specially sent representatives to Shanghai last month to conduct peace talks. Regarding the convening of the Fourth National Congress, the Ning and Guangdong parties initially had their own claims. Finally, it was decided that the Fourth National Congress would be held separately in Ning and Guangdong with a spirit of cooperation. Since the Fourth National Congress had the claim of uniting comrades from the First, Second, and Third Congresses, the First Conference of the Fourth Central Executive and Supervisory Committee could fundamentally seek a solution to the party and government. The First Conference of the Fourth National Congress can be called the Unification Conference. At the First Conference of the Fourth National Congress, the responsibility of reorganizing the government should naturally be borne. There are many crises in the party and the country now. The comrades of the Fourth National Congress of our party should bear the responsibility of restoring the faith of our party. If our party has no way to do it after today, not only will the people's hope for the party be lost, but our party will also be difficult to continue to survive. We are opening the Fourth National Congress at this critical juncture, and its significance is more important than any previous Congress. The only responsibility in the future is to first engage in internal party unity, restore party rights, and rebuild revolutionary forces, and then we can secure the country and resist foreign aggression. Then Chen Jitang gave a speech, briefly saying that the opening of today's Fourth National Congress is a new opportunity for the party. If we want to restore the party's strength, we must first be united. The way to unite must be to establish [common trust], [mutual trust], [mutual understanding], and [mutual love]. If we can be united in spirit, then this department can be revived and developed. Regarding politics, we should overthrow the dictatorship and build a permanent civilian government. Regarding the economy, we should proceed according to the National Founding Strategy and the National Founding Outline. Regarding elections, comrades must stand in the party's position, seek talents for the party, and not have personal emotional effects. After the speech, the cannons were fired and the music was played, and the ceremony was completed. At 11:30, photos were taken and the meeting was adjourned. It was decided that a preparatory meeting would be held at 2:00 p.m. on the 19th. It was heard that the conference period would be set for ten days (November 18th evening)

Anti-Japanese Association Sets Deadline for Sealing Japanese Goods The Wuxian Anti-Japanese Association has set a deadline of the 24th for all stores to seal up all Japanese goods. If Japanese goods are found, they will be treated as smuggling of Japanese goods. The County Chamber of Commerce has notified all industries yesterday to each nominate three people within three days to jointly conduct the inspection.

Yangzhou 68

After the Punishment of Traitorous Merchants Various Shapes and Colors Since the implementation of confiscating inferior goods in stores and punishing traitorous merchants and merchants' strikes by the People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of this county, the Anti-Japanese Association executed the punishment of traitorous merchants standing in wooden cages yesterday, and the situation has become more tense. In the past two days, only merchants related to inferior goods were on strike, and the doors were still plastered with strips of paper saying [Stop business, distinguish Japanese goods separately] and [Negotiate methods for distinguishing Japanese goods]. But starting this morning (22nd), all industries in the city were on strike. The paper strips written on the doors of the relevant industries have been torn off. If small merchants are found not to be on strike, they will be persuaded to stop business by their colleagues. As a result, the market has suddenly become desolate. Hundreds of merchants have gathered at the Chamber of Commerce, waiting for Zhu, the standing committee member and executive director of the representatives who went to the province to petition, to return to Yangzhou to report the results of the petition. It is also heard that the provincial party and government organs have assigned a committee member who will come to Yangzhou with Zhu and others to investigate the truth and resolve everything. However, each trade association, with Wang Jingting, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, attending the Anti-Japanese Association on behalf of the business community, was recommended to serve as a standing committee member. It is heard that the Anti-Japanese Association cannot accommodate Wang's representative to speak for the merchants, and specially sent a letter to the Anti-Japanese Association to withdraw the representative immediately, and stated that the business community will not send representatives to attend future meetings. It is also known that there were slogans found in the streets and markets this morning that were written by merchants who were wronged, [Chairman Wang secretly used conspiracy and did not strive for the wronged people with the Anti-Japanese Association, but allowed them to be slaughtered, and did not sincerely act as the master for the merchants], etc. In addition, Zhou Liren and other shop assistants of the cloth industry, because the owners were affected by the sealing of inferior goods, were afraid that the economic turnover would not be活, and they would not be able to resolve the strike. They were afraid that if the business was suspended, the labor would have no means of living. Therefore, all the shop assistants held a meeting today and decided to petition the Chamber of Commerce to quickly seek a solution. Regarding the inferior goods of the industry, they requested that the shop assistants be allowed to seal them up on behalf of the owners, and prohibit them from continuing to import them. If the owners are found to be secretly importing them again, the labor will report to the Chamber of Commerce and forward them to the Anti-Japanese Association for punishment. In order to prevent the labor and the capital from colluding, the labor is allowed to expel the person involved from membership, and prohibit them from serving in the 塲 forever.

Mid-Voyage Robbery of Huzhou-Hangzhou Boat: The No. 3 night boat traveling from this city to Hangzhou was sailing near Mao Song Bridge in Deqing County at approximately 9:00 PM on the 20th of this month when a bandit boat suddenly appeared. Therefore, at approximately 10:00 AM on the 22nd, Chief Prosecutor Pan Yinting supervised the extraction of the criminal, confirmed his identity, and escorted him to the South School Field in this city for execution.

Educational News

Important News

Jiangsu Province: Middle School Education Fee Issue 71

The Important Reason for Financial Strain

Remedial Measures by the Executive Committee

Bearing the Pain in the Face of National Crisis

The Executive Committee of the Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Teachers' Association sent a letter to various provincial schools, stating: "Regarding the fact that since the beginning of the academic year, almost four months have passed, and only half a month's worth of education fees have been issued, we, who were hired, are not responsible for raising funds. However, those in administrative positions neglect their duties and only know how to be officials, not how to do things. Who else is affected by this besides us? Investigating the reasons for the financial strain on education fees, the important reasons are as follows: (1) The Ministry of Finance has not repaid any of the debt. Before 1927, the cigarette tax revenue was used for Jiangsu Province's education fees. Since 1927, the cigarette tax revenue has been returned to the Ministry of Finance, and 1.8 million yuan was allocated from the land tax to offset this, with an agreement at the time that any shortfall would be made up by the Ministry of Finance. However, since 1927, there has been an annual shortfall of about 600,000 yuan, and the cigarette tax rate has been increased year by year. Over the past four years, the total shortfall in land tax has been more than 2.5 million yuan. Despite repeated demands, the Ministry of Finance ignores them. This is one reason. (2) Unreasonable occupation of National Central University's funding. The annual expenditure for National Central University is 1.32 million yuan, accounting for about half of the province's education fees. However, according to the budget expenditure standards promulgated by the National Government's Accounting Office in 1930, it is clearly stipulated that the funding for national schools should be paid by the state, and the land tax should be allocated for local use. Furthermore, the slaughter tax is designated as a local tax. Therefore, the funding for National Central University should undoubtedly be paid by the national treasury. In addition, Jiangsu Province suffered a major flood this year, and tax revenue has decreased sharply. The province's own schools are on the verge of running out of funds, making it even more difficult to bear the expenses of national schools. For several years, despite the association's efforts to stop the payments, the committee refused to sign. As of the beginning of this month, the Jiangsu Education Fee Committee held its 26th meeting and still decided to allocate the Ministry of Finance's recent subsidy of 600,000 yuan to National Central University, while the remaining 720,000 yuan would still be provided by Jiangsu Province, an illegal occupation. This is the second reason." On November 18th, the Jiangsu Provincial Education Fee Committee held its 26th meeting at the Education Department to discuss remedial measures. Here is a record of what was heard at the time: "(A) The annual education fee for the entire province is about 4.8 million yuan, and the old debt is about 800,000 yuan, totaling 5.6 million yuan. (B) (1) Ministry of Finance subsidy: 600,000 yuan (2) New subsidy: 600,000 yuan (already used by National Central University) (3) Provincial government subsidy: 300,000 yuan (4) New provincial government subsidy: 300,000 yuan (half of the Shata income) (5) School accommodation fees: 200,000 yuan (6) Education Management Office loan: 300,000 yuan (7) Actual receipt: 2.5 million yuan (8) Issuance of public bonds: about 600,000 yuan, totaling 5.6 million yuan. If the above subsidy measures can be fully implemented, it may not be a method of relief. However, whether this can be achieved in reality is still a very big question. Now, the funding is in arrears for three months, and what will happen in the future is unknown. However, in this time of national crisis, we have to temporarily bear the pain. Regarding the resolution of the 9th Representative Congress to convene an all-powers representative conference of various schools by the Executive Committee when necessary, we will observe the national situation and then determine our course of action. We hope to receive your valuable insights. This is addressed to the Middle School Teachers' Association for your perusal."

Representatives of University and Middle School Students 73

At 9 AM, students from various universities will hold demonstrations in the South City and Zhabei districts. The Student Union has already made all the necessary arrangements. This petition seems to be more planned and organized than the previous one. The university delegation and the middle school delegation both held very important meetings yesterday afternoon. The details are recorded below:

(1) University Delegation 74

The university delegation to Beijing convened its third meeting at the Youth Propaganda Group yesterday afternoon at 1 PM. Zhou Xiaobo chaired the meeting, and Zheng Yizhi served as the recorder. Each school reported the number of people going to Beijing, approximately 8,000 people.

Various Important Proposals Were Resolved: (1) Gather at the North Station and depart at 3 PM on the 24th (i.e., today). (C) Secretary: Jiaoguang, Soochow, Political Science. (D) Director of General Affairs Department: Gaochuan; Accountant: Wenhua; Business: Jiangnan, Daxia. (E) Public Relations Department: Liangjiang (full-time); Law School, Chinese Medicine College. (2) Perseverance and hard work. (3) Mutual assistance. (4) Neat formation. (5) Clean attire. (6) Simple luggage. (7) No leaving the ranks without permission. (8) No rushing to take seats. (9) No arbitrary talking and laughing. (10) No randomly expressing opinions. All members of our association, filled with righteous indignation, went to Beijing to petition for resisting the enemy and avenging our humiliation in late September. Today, Heilongjiang Province has fallen, and Tianjin City is being disturbed. The Japanese invaders are becoming more ferocious, and the League of Nations is in despair. The government has violated its promise and has not shown any actual troop deployment. Now, our association is heartbroken and feels that the country's demise is imminent. This mission is extremely important. The delegation to Beijing will maintain a highly disciplined spirit and a firm attitude. Before the government shows actual troop deployment, the delegation, entrusted by all Shanghai students, will not leave Beijing without permission. We hope that national compatriots will recognize our sincere intentions and rise up to help us. The future of the nation truly depends on it. Jointly declared by the Shanghai University Students Anti-Japanese National Salvation United Association.

Declaration by the Shanghai University Joint Association 76

At 3 PM on the 22nd of this month, the Shanghai University Joint Association held a general meeting at the Great China Restaurant due to the seriousness of the situation. Representatives from 19 schools, including Labor, Chizhi, China Public, Jiaotong, Tongji, East Asia Physical Education College, Shanghai Fine Arts College, Datong, Fazheng, Jinan, Guanghua, Sino-French, China University Business College, Soochow, Fudan, Music College, Daxia, Hujiang, and Shanghai Law School, attended. President Li of Jiaotong University chaired the meeting and passed resolutions on the declaration (see below), telegram to Shi Zhaoji urging to prioritize troop withdrawal, and the organization of a lecture tour and a national university joint association. The meeting adjourned at 6:30 PM.

Declaration: The faculty and staff of the Shanghai University Joint Association rarely discuss politics on ordinary days. However, with a strong enemy pressing on the border and the country in imminent danger, the government authorities, in terms of military affairs, fold their arms and sit idly by, watching the fall of the Northeast; in terms of diplomacy, trust in the natural changes of the League of Nations; and in terms of internal affairs, the realization of a unified government is nowhere in sight. All three of these points are related to the survival of our country and nation. We have to discuss them with our countrymen to the best of our understanding. Recently, Provincial Chairman Ma Zhanshan defended against the violence with a lone army, washing away the shame of the fleeing armies of Liaoning and Jilin. His reputation spread, and the whole country was moved. However, he eventually abandoned Longjiang due to a lack of supplies and support. Our country raises an army of two million, spending 28 million yuan per month, but those who hold military power value their own territories, are indifferent to the suffering of others, and do not care about them. The war against Russia on the Middle East Railway is clear evidence of this. Now that the three northeastern provinces have fallen, the commander-in-chief of the military forces has only begun to talk about going north. We believe that it is the duty of soldiers to resist the enemy when they come, and they should act promptly without hesitation. As for deploying defenses and raising funds, they have not had time to borrow them, even after two months. Going to the rescue today is already too late. Not going today is deceiving the people and selling out the country. This is the first point regarding military affairs. Representative Shi Zhaoji has tried his best to mediate, but his instructions are actually within the country. When the League of Nations adjourns, it is the time for our country to calmly discuss and resolve internal disputes, without having time to pay attention to others. Looking back at Japan, Uchimura resigned from his post in the United States, and Matsudaira lobbied in England. When the meeting reopens, the odds are set. Compared to them, we are naturally inferior. Now that the League of Nations has failed to reconcile, and the violent Japanese continue to advance, we did not start the conflict, so why talk about a truce? The Japanese conspiracy has been completely exposed, so what is the use of investigation? As for not ordering the Japanese to withdraw their troops and sending an investigation team first, and expanding the scope of the investigation, our country should reject them all. Our country should especially quickly and decisively invoke Articles 15 and 16 of the League of Nations Covenant, present them to the League of Nations, and quickly impose further sanctions to urge Japan to withdraw its troops, and formally appeal to the signatory countries of the Washington Treaty to support public opinion. This is the second point regarding diplomacy. Comrades of the Kuomintang are fighting and scolding each other, cutting themselves off from the masses, but the masses still cannot bear to abandon them. When the Unity and Peace Conference was held in Shanghai, we thought that the comrades could truly repent of their mistakes, unite, forgive the past, and plan for the future, calling for success and establishing a unified government immediately to appease the country and resist foreign aggression. Who knew that after more than ten days of turmoil, the result was only a four-plenary session that separated the two regions. This is the bitter intention of the comrades in the party who are unwilling to openly break up. At this time, we cannot demand too much, but we ask the comrades in both regions to work together, quickly eliminate all prejudices, limit the organization of a unified government, to appease the masses. A promise is worth a thousand pieces of gold, and the hope of extinction. This is the third point regarding internal affairs. All three of these points are major issues, and other matters will not be discussed in detail today. At this time, when internal and external troubles are pressing on us, the national sentiment is indignant and high, and the four peoples have suspended their studies and are running around to find a way to survive. This is what is proper and reasonable, and no laws can prohibit it. If those who hold the reins of power, give a loud call and rise up to resist foreign aggression, taking the will of the people as their own will, then the people will follow closely, like a shadow, without having to seek the peace of the people, and the people will be peaceful by themselves, without having to seek the trust of the people, and the people will trust by themselves. Having gained the trust of the people, to unanimously resist foreign aggression, what is there to fear from foreign enemies? Why are the people so fond of Ma Zhanshan, but willing to help him, because he can defend the country and resist foreign aggression and trust him. As for the fundamental plan, it lies in education. We are willing to share the responsibility with the government, and once the situation has stabilized, we will contribute our humble opinions for consideration. We hereby declare.

Shanghai Education Bureau's Patriotic Activities: Postponement of the Deadline for Essay Contest 77

Results of the Preliminary Rounds for Elementary School Groups 1 and 2 Announced

The patriotic activity achievement competition held by the Education Bureau is divided into three parts: achievement exhibition, essay contest, and speech contest. It is reported that after the essay contest was revised, there are preliminary, semi-final, and final rounds. It is hoped that all schools in this city will widely participate. The previously set date was too tight, and it was feared that schools in rural areas would not be able to respond in time. Therefore, it has been decided to postpone the deadline by several days. The preparatory committee has decided to change the deadline for essay submission to November 30, and all schools have been notified.

Also, the preliminary rounds for elementary school groups 1 and 2 were held on the 20th and 21st, respectively.
